    Configuration options

    EARLY_PRINTK enabled PREEMPT_RT_BASE enabled

    Problem description

    mpdecision is causing problems. mpdecision is like cpufreq utilities but is specific for Qualcomm processors, and is a closed binary.

    Solution

    Disable mpdecision initialization in the init.hammerhead.rc script in the ramdisk image.
